Sports News

All Proceeds from Qiu Fei Memorial Tournament Remitted to Qiu's Family Yesterday – Totaling 463.5 Yuan in National Currency, Xinhua Offers Free Remittance – Only Over Ten Yuan Received for Memorial Cup Donations to Date – Qiu's Family Still Overseas, Hu Xiansheng Appeals for Assistance

Tennis elder Hu Xiansheng, saddened by the death of our national tennis player Qiu Feihai in a foreign land, mourned the demise of a national athlete and the drifting of the weak. He initiated the Qiu Feihai Memorial Tennis Tournament in order to raise funds to help Qiu's family. He received the sympathy of the Western Grassland Association of Wusong and the French Chamber of Commerce, and the tournament was held at the French Chamber of Commerce courts on the previous Saturday. It raised over 400 yuan. The details were reported in the previous newspaper. Later, Mr. Hu was unable to remit the funds because he did not know the address of Qiu's family. According to Mr. Hu, after days of inquiry, he obtained accurate information from Mr. Lin Baohua yesterday morning. Qiu's wife had sent a letter to Mr. Lin the day before, saying that she and her mother were still drifting in Penang and asked for assistance. Only then did he know the exact location of Qiu's family. Yesterday, all the proceeds from the tickets, minus the formal expenses incurred by the French Chamber of Commerce for the competition, were remitted by Xinhua Savings Bank to Qiu's family in Penang, totaling 463.5 yuan in national currency. Mr. Chen Bugao, manager of the Xinhua Xifayuan Branch, was very sympathetic and volunteered to help without charging any remittance fees. This also shows Mr. Chen's righteousness. The Qiu Feihai Memorial Cup Competition has been fundraising for a week since it started. Yesterday, this person (Hu referring to himself) specifically inquired at the Xinhua Bank on Xifayuan Road, the collection point for donations. However, only over ten yuan had been received to date. It is hoped that people from all walks of life will sympathize with Qiu's plight and contribute generously so that the annual memorial trophy can be held as scheduled, so as to commemorate a great figure in the tennis world, and the remaining funds can be remitted a second time to subsidize Qiu's family's future life and return expenses. According to reports, the Qiu Memorial Cup Competition was initiated by Mr. Hu Xiansheng. His plan is to use 250 yuan from the donations to make a silver cup, and the remainder will still be remitted to Qiu's family. The Memorial Cup will be managed by a committee organized by the National Sports Association. The competition will be held annually, and the winner will keep it for one year. Following the model of the 台杯(Taiwan Cup) method, the cup is engraved. In addition to Qiu's wife, Qiu's family also has an elderly mother in her seventies and a minor girl, all of whom are old and weak.

Small Ball Brawl at the Chinese Association

The Chinese Small Ball Association, organizer of the Sino-Association League Cup, held a total of eight fierce matches yesterday. In one match, the Kang team faced the Shanghai Eagle team, but the Shanghai Eagle team forfeited, giving the Kang team an easy win. (The Shanghai Eagle team has forfeited twice, and the association has revoked their qualification for the competition.) In another match between the Mubei Star team and the Weiguang team, an unfortunate incident occurred. In the first half, the Weiguang team scored two consecutive goals, leaving the North Star team scoreless, which inevitably led to rough play. After the Weiguang team scored another goal, several hundred spectators supporting the North Star team became inexplicably angry, and the atmosphere in the stadium became tense. Qin Zhirui, a player from the North Star team, eager to win, recklessly attacked and was blocked by Liang Bingyan of the Weiguang team. Qin then acted illegally, and the referee Zhang Zhixiang ordered him off the field. Qin Zhirui not only disobeyed the referee but also became very stubborn. Some spectators supporting the North Star team shouted to hit the referee and swarmed onto the field. After the spectators were ordered to leave, play resumed. Jin Minglai of the North Star team shot fiercely at Liang Bingyan's side. Liang was injured and fell to the ground and kicked at Jin. Several hundred spectators supporting the North Star team rushed onto the field and attacked. Liang Bingyan was severely beaten and humiliated and fled the field. Spectators chased after him, but Huang Yitian of the association stepped in to stop them. The North Star team, realizing they were in the wrong, held a meeting that evening at the Jinlan Restaurant and decided that the North Star team had violated the rules of small ball, and their membership was revoked. Liang Bingyan of the Weiguang team was also disqualified for overstepping the line.

Accompanying the World Games Delegation (13th Letter) Special Correspondent Feng Youzhen Sent by the Central News Agency

The Battle of Norway and Poland

First half: Two to two

Second half: One to zero

Result: Three to two

Norway wins

The Norwegian and Polish teams, having been defeated by Italy and Austria respectively, competed at 4 p.m. on the 13th to determine third and fourth place. Over 100,000 spectators watched from the sidelines. The strength of the two teams can be described as evenly matched, each with its own strengths. Poland's front line is extremely sharp, with fast and accurate wingers, which are rare to see. However, their shooting technique is lacking, and they miss good opportunities at critical moments. The center and back lines are also very strong, saving many dangerous balls. The Norwegian team has average talent across the board, but they do not panic in the face of battle and have a strong fighting spirit, which is their distinguishing characteristic. Therefore, they were able to complete the victory in the final moments. The lineups of the two teams are as follows:

Norway: Holmboe, Bestad, Johoem, Sheng Flanchden, Najov, Martinsen, Sheng Ericson, Quanmen, Ulburg, Monsen

Poland: Da Tuo, Ke Aponski, Qie Lixisi, Sipongnik, Jie Bolage, Lage La Gao Te, Bert Locke, Man Nia Si, Hua Leqiang Referee: Birlem (Germany), Linesmen: Petere (Germany), Eglrew (Sweden)

Poland Takes the Lead. The bell rings four times, and the two teams in military uniform take the field, each occupying one side. They shoot, exercise, and loosen their muscles. The referee summons the captains to shake hands and make peace. The coin is tossed to determine position, and the war breaks out immediately. Poland makes the first move, and Jof refuses to accept the invitation. Martinsen gets the ball and advances, and Jie Bolage also clings on. You come and I go, all in vain, wasting their efforts. At ten minutes, Poland sneaks in from the right. Hua Leqiang wants to make a fancy play, but Holmboe is actually stumped. He passes the ball to the center with one kick. Man Tuo Yasi's foot steps on it. Ling Mussen steps forward to grab it. Man Tuo Yasi hooks it back. Hua Da Si rushes up and shoots fiercely. Jona Sheng has no way to save it. The Polish team opens the scoring first. The four seats shout in unison, shaking the earth. The Polish team is not satisfied and continues to invade, killing the Norwegian team so that they only have the power to parry and no power to fight back. At thirteen minutes, Gao Te raises the banner of righteousness in front of the goal. Holm Sheng is forced to do nothing but make it a corner kick. Hua Leqiang kicks it in just right. Jona Sheng has to lift it upwards, over the crossbar. Hua Leqiang kicks another corner kick. Eric Sheng shouts loudly, rushes forward to block it. Bert Locke intercepts it and aims at the goal, shooting fiercely. Jona Sheng bends over to welcome the guests, catching it head-on. However, the momentum is too strong, and he slips to the ground. Fortunately, he is agile and immediately picks it up and kicks it out. The Norwegian forwards are not useless. At twenty-five minutes, they receive support from the defenders. With a command, they have already swarmed to the Polish city. Martinsen initially fires a heavy cannon, but it fails to blossom. Seeing the left side empty, he lightly passes it out. Bestad rushes up and kicks it, directly into the upper right corner. Aponski cannot resist. One to one, the score is tied. The Norwegian team has won the first battle, and the front-line soldiers are even more active. Six minutes later, they pass forward and point their spears directly at the goal. Bestad receives support from Martinsen and shoots again on the left side, breaking the net. The two goals before and after are played the same way. Two to one, Norway comes from behind. The Polish army is enraged and retaliates. Three minutes later, Hua Da Si dribbles forward, directly to the Norwegian goal. Just as he is about to raise his foot to shoot, he suddenly slips and falls. Hua Da Si is quick-witted and takes advantage of the situation. Bert Locke flies up and catches up. Foot up, ball down. Two to two, another tie. From then on, the situation becomes increasingly tense. Although both sides have repeated turbulence, they do not lose an inch of land. The first half ends, and everyone is in a good mood.

Norway Wins in the End

After the break, the Norwegian army's momentum suddenly surges, and their brilliance is revealed. At eight minutes, the central army, led by Ma Liao Sheng, penetrates deep, passes several times, and then fires a direct shot, sharp and powerful. Unfortunately, it hits the goalpost and bounces out, and his ambitions are not fulfilled. The Polish team counterattacks, and Gao Te also makes a wild shot. After that, Norway had three shooting opportunities. The first time, the center forward was Ding Sheng, who kicked hard from ten yards in front of the goal, but it flew into the sky. The second time, Martinsen again got the ball from the upper yards in front of the goal, with no obstruction in front, but he launched it a little late and was rescued by Sipongnik. The third time, Martinsen again swept the ball on the ground in front of the goal, but it was caught by Aponski. Conversely, the Polish side also had several chances to win, but they all missed the opportunity and failed to achieve anything. In a fierce battle, it was thought that extra time would be needed to determine the winner. Who knew that one bell before the end, Norway sneaked in from the right. The Polish right back, Qie Lixisi, stepped forward to grab it and slipped. Monsen quickly passed it to Martinsen. Martinsen deliberately made a gap. Hua Da Si rushed up and kicked hard, sharp and powerful. Aponski jumped up to block it, but the ball still bounced into the goalpost. Although Poland's ambition did not die, after two or three passes, the whistle blew long, and Norway won the final victory by three to two. (End of letter 12)

Education News

Sino-British Gengkuan Board Plans to Develop Education in the Northwest; Mei Yibao and Others Go to Lanzhou for Inspection

Lanzhou Air Express, In order to develop education in the Northwest, the Sino-British Gengkuan Board has specially allocated 200,000 yuan from the educational and cultural undertakings subsidy fund for the 25th year to subsidize primary and secondary school education in the four provinces of Gansu, Qinghai, Ningxia, and Suiyuan. The detailed measures must be determined concretely after sending personnel to the west for investigation. Therefore, Dai Liren, a British national who is a director of the Sino-British Gengkuan Board and a professor at Yanjing University, Mei Yibao, the academic dean of Yanjing University, Guo Youshou, a special commissioner of the Ministry of Education, and assistants Li Mengying and Bai Baojin were organized into the Northwest Education Inspection Group of the Sino-British Gengkuan Board to conduct on-the-spot inspections in the Northwest. Li and Bai had already arrived in Lanzhou from Shaanxi a few days ago. Mei and his party of three flew from Ningxia to this question at noon on the 9th and stayed at the Lanzhou Lizhi Branch. According to Mei's conversation with the reporter, the Sino-British Gengkuan Board, in order to have a solid basis when distributing the four northwestern educational funds, has organized this group. They departed from Peiping to Suiyuan, inspected for two weeks, and have a preliminary understanding of the current educational situation in the province and the social needs for education. Although the inspection in Ningxia lasted only one week, they thoroughly investigated all important areas. The purpose of coming to Lanzhou is, of course, to focus on educational inspections, but it is also necessary to attach importance to the social economy and people's livelihood that are related to education, so as to serve as a reference for future distribution of collaborative funds. The original date was set for two weeks, and the event will immediately go to Qinghai. At the moment, everything related has not been discussed with Chairman Yu and Director Tian, so it is still undecided how many days are needed in Gansu and whether they will be able to go to Qinghai in the future. (September 12)

New Rules for Managing Players of the Newcastle Football Team in England: Must Return to the Team Before 10:30 PM; Dancing Prohibited Four Days Before the Game

Reuters London: The Newcastle football team has set some new rules for managing players this season, which are very interesting. Here are the highlights: (1) Must return to the team before 10:30 pm two nights before the game; (2) Dancing is prohibited four days before each game; (3) Unless specially allowed by the trainer, players are not allowed to drink alcohol on the train when traveling for away games; (4) The club is not responsible for accidents if players drive cars.

Measures to Increase Funding for Free Education in Various County-level Cities in Zhejiang Province: Discretionary Income from Autonomous Surcharges

The self-raised funding for free education in each county-level city in Zhejiang Province in the previous year lacked reliable methods, which inevitably affected the progress of the undertaking. This year, it is planned to increase revenue from the autonomous household donations in each county-level city to ensure a definite and consistent source of funding for free education. The specific measures are as follows: (1) The funding for implementing short-term compulsory education in each county-level city, starting from the 25th year, should be collected together with the autonomous surcharges. (2) For county-level cities where autonomous surcharges have already been approved, the amount should be increased by 10% to 35% of the autonomous household donations, taking into account actual needs. The percentage should be reported to the three bureaus of Civil Affairs, Finance, and Education for approval on a case-by-case basis. (3) For county-level cities where autonomous surcharges are being submitted for approval or have not been approved, the three bureaus of Civil Affairs, Finance, and Education will consider the actual needs of each county-level city and approve the increase percentage on a case-by-case basis. In addition, each county-level city may, with approval, allocate funds from (1) late payment penalties for field tax county tax, (2) slaughter surcharges, and (3) collection of old taxes belonging to the county tax portion, and instruct them to be implemented separately.

Memorial Service for Zhang Taiyan Held by the Educational Community in Sichuan on the 27th at Sichuan University. The 27th at Sichuan University

Ren Hongjun, President of Sichuan University, Zhang Linggao, President of West China University, He Xiaoqi, former Director of the Sichuan Education Department, and more than one hundred people from the education community, including Meng Shouchun, Luo Zhongshu, Deng Xugong, Xiang Chu, Li Zhi, Li Weifen, Chen Peide, Zhang Yi, and Pang Jun, will hold a memorial service for Mr. Zhang Taiyan at Zhigongtang, Sichuan University in Chengdu on the 27th of this month. The public announcement is recorded as follows: "We hereby respectfully announce that Mr. Zhang Taiyan of Yuhang, with his extraordinary talent, was in a position of obscurity. In the early years of turmoil, his dragon-like virtue was hidden. He retired to write books and lecture, presiding over the atmosphere for over forty years. This summer in June, he passed away in Suzhou. The court and the countryside, far and near, rushed to mourn, because the existence and death of this person is of great importance to the national scholarship of China, not just a private concern of one time and one place. We and other colleagues had long admired his righteousness and had either participated in the last seats of the allusions or entrusted ourselves to the slight contract of private learning. Mountains and rivers obstruct the funeral, so we can only hold a memorial service at Zhigongtang, Sichuan University in Chengdu on September 27th. All of us countrymen, who share the same spirit, feel grief for the death of a person and the decline of the country. It is hoped that we can mourn the division of Taoism and the withering of the philosopher, and that we can come together to express our condolences, so that we can believe that our Tao is not alone and that we can rise up and inherit our noble virtues. This is what we aspire to. We respectfully announce, and hope you will understand."

Appointment Orders from the Municipal Education Bureau for Chairpersons of Primary Education Research Associations in Various Districts

August Raw Silk Export Report: Exports Decreased Sharply... Market Conditions Were Weak

According to the report from the Commodity Inspection Bureau of the Ministry of Industries, in August, the export of Chinese silk to the Americas was 1,300 bales, to Europe 1,490 bales, to Africa 321 bales, and to Asia 193 bales. By category, the export of white factory silk was 2,637 bales, Tussah and White Soil silk 200 bales, Yellow Factory silk 5 bales, Yellow Warp and Yellow Soil silk 276 bales, Gray Warp 64 bales, and Douppion silk 122 bales. In addition, the export of waste silk was 2,926 bales. Since the new silk season began this year (starting in June), the total export of Chinese silk in three months was 16,090 bales, a decrease of 5,670 bales compared to 21,760 bales in the same period last year.

The silk market was initially stable in August, but then became weak due to sluggish foreign sales. Silk prices therefore fell frequently. For several months, the domestic silk market has been affected by the fluctuating markets in New York and Yokohama, with foreign cables consistently differing from domestic market prices by a huge 30-50 yuan, causing the market atmosphere to often be deadlocked. Fortunately, domestic sales were still active, and general sentiment was unusually enthusiastic. Although sales from foreign firms were not strong, market prices were still able to hold steady, and the foundation seemed quite stable. Entering August, foreign firms continued to present a deadlocked situation, causing general sentiment to worry about the future. In addition, this month was the period for the settlement of large commodity futures, and actual sales from foreign firms remained stagnant, with long positions crowded in the market, and the market atmosphere became increasingly sluggish. However, according to general observation, if European and American sales can be activated, there is hope that the market will recover.

Special Feature Answer to Mr. Ding Renjun of the Bangbu Yixing Company

(1) Liverpool (i.e., Hanmai): Each unit is a "peck," weighing 112 pounds. Twenty pecks make a ton (i.e., 2240 pounds), equivalent to 2032 catties in the market scale.

Chicago (i.e., American wheat): Each unit is a "bushel," weighing 60 pounds. 33.33 bushels make a ton (i.e., 2000 pounds), equivalent to 1814.24 catties in the market scale. Canada is the same.

(2) The prices of British and American gold exchanges published in the newspaper are calculated based on one or one hundred national currency units. Conversion can be done accordingly.

(3) The cost of ordering foreign wheat sometimes fluctuates. According to common practice, when a deal is made, it is based on CIFC, which includes freight, insurance, and the agreed-upon wheat price. The ordering party only needs to inspect and receive the goods at the unloading location. As for FOB, it only covers up to the loading of the ship at the wheat production site, excluding other expenses. The difference between CIFC and FOB is about seventeen shillings per ton. The choice between the two depends entirely on the ordering party's preference. The transportation costs and freight can be deduced from these figures for clarity.

(4) The market prices of foreign wheat are all standard. The situation is similar to the standards of our country's exchange. Because the quality of the spot goods varies, the pricing is naturally different. It is like the wheat in our country, where the market value sometimes exceeds the standard and sometimes it is the opposite. Even for various spot goods, the difference between high and low prices can be three to five jiao. Therefore, operators should understand the names but not necessarily the actual quality.

(5) Regarding inquiries, the author has tried to provide detailed answers within a possible scope. However, there is no need to answer trivial matters. Your understanding is appreciated.

Wenzhou Route

Haiyan: 16

Large Arrival of Foreign Indica Rice Still Causes Price Stagnation

Yesterday, the arrival volume of foreign indica rice remained high, with ample stock in the market. The source of supply continued unabated, and shipments kept arriving. Hence, merchants were rather anxious and sought to sell at extremely low prices. Yesterday, buyers from Guangdong province became active again, and the market suddenly livened up. 14,000 bags of unpolished Hankou rice were sold, all purchased by Guangdong buyers. Buyers from Shantou also had a strong appetite, invigorating business on this street. However, as merchants were eager to sell, prices could not rise significantly. If the rate of sales continues to be strong, then the market may improve. Yesterday's shipments included over 2,000 bags of Jiangxi rice, 1,200 bags of Hunan rice, 14,000 bags of unpolished Hankou rice, 600 bags of unpolished Jiangbei rice, and 2,000 bags of Guangdong indica rice.

No Improvement in Sales of Heshia Rice

(South Shanghai) Yesterday, the source of goods from various groups was limited to numbers 12 and 13, totaling 2,400 to 2,500 piculs. Retail sales remained sluggish. Qingdao Dasu buyers purchased 500 to 600 bags of thin early japonica rice. Consequently, the price of thick early japonica rice continued to decline. The price of thin rice was fixed. Dongxin japonica rice experienced no rise or fall. Xin Yanglu and other top grades decreased slightly by five cents. Yinbianyuan remained at the same price.

(North Shanghai) Yesterday, the Heshia rice supply came from numbers 34 and 35. Merchants sold various types of rice at a small profit to expedite sales. The market showed a slight increase for high-quality broken japonica rice. Medium and lower grades decreased by one or two cents. Xin Yangjian rice saw a sharp decline of two or three cents. Xinbujian, Yinbianyuan, thin rice, and Chen Yangjian also decreased slightly by a few cents to about one cent. Xin Tuanjian rice sold at the same price. The prices of Dongxi Xin japonica rice were similar. Xin Kejian rice prices weakened by nearly one cent.

The Authority of the Chef (Part 1)

— Huang Yiqing

(5) Power of Life and Death in Their Hands

"If someone gets sick from eating my food, it's the same as me getting sick. I would lose face." This was said by a German working for a German manager, Woolefu, who was the manager of the Qingdao Ti Du Lou hotel. Therefore, he urged all chefs and technicians to maintain cleanliness to the utmost degree. Even the cooking pots had to be scrubbed with sandpaper every night to make them bright and new; using ordinary furnace ash was considered too dirty. "Treating others' hunger as one's own," "Treating others' drowning as one's own," a chef with such a demeanor shows the sense of responsibility and national morality of people from that country.

In fact, let's recall: "So-and-so died from eating a certain meal and getting sick," such statements are often heard. During the years of the Republic of China (1919-1920), when a certain school in Hangzhou was disturbed by a case of poison in the rice pot, the authority of the chef was naturally felt to be particularly great. An American elementary school health book stated, "The chef's job is more important than most lawyers, doctors, civil servants, and teachers," which is absolutely correct. Because: indeed! If a chef is even slightly careless, and some pathogenic organisms contaminate the food, it might end the life of the homeowner or customer. In other words, acts of "hiding a sword in the fish" can be seen everywhere in society, and no one should consider it the special province of Zhuan Zhu.

In our country's autocratic era, the phrase "salt and plums" in cooking was used to metaphorically refer to managing the world and governing with deliberation. However, in the past, we only knew that it was important in the positive sense, especially in terms of flavoring and promoting appetite. Now that health principles have become clear, three major negative responsibilities have been added to the chef and cook's role. One is the control of food components, which must be properly controlled so that the people who eat it are sufficiently nourished and do not suffer from malnutrition or various nutrient deficiencies. One is the guarantee of food hygiene, which must be properly guaranteed so that the people who eat it do not suffer from various dirty diseases and intestinal parasitic diseases. The other is the easily digestible preparation of food, which must be prepared carefully so that the people who eat it do not suffer from digestive problems or indigestion. Among these, the second is the most serious and urgent.

To avoid accidental errors in the second aspect, the author has two very common secrets to share with my respected chefs! At the same time, I would like to ask those who employ chefs to pay attention to checking them!

One is called "fire to the point where the pig's head is tender"; the other is called "old but not wrong, is clean."

From the Failure of the Olympic Games to Full Body Health Checkups

— Gu Honglie

The Olympic Games held in Berlin, Germany, in August of this year can be described as a competition for national health. Whoever has a healthy and great physique has the best chance of winning the championship. The athletes attending from various countries are all elite athletes from their respective countries. When our country's athletes were sent abroad, we fully expected them to win championships and bring honor to the motherland. Who knew that from the opening to the closing ceremony, news came that athletes from various countries had won gold, silver, and bronze medals, while our country returned empty-handed? Wags said that we got a big duck egg. Some blamed our country's athletes for not fighting hard enough, but in reality, the decisive injury in our country's failure in the Olympic Games was a physique that was not great and strength that was inferior to others. We cannot ignore the facts and falsely accuse the athletes. According to historical statistics, the physique of the Chinese people is gradually shrinking, and at the same time, life expectancy is gradually decreasing. Compared with our eastern neighbor Japan, which was often called a short country in the past, in recent decades, because the government authorities have paid attention to national health and implemented healthy marriages, the physique of the people in that country has become stronger and stronger from generation to generation, and life expectancy has also become longer and longer from generation to generation. Therefore, if our entire country does not pay attention to health checkups and healthy marriages, and even knowingly marries someone who has a disease that can be passed on to future generations because of status, the saying goes, "You reap what you sow." It is a natural principle that the descendants passed down by unhealthy partners will certainly not be healthy. If the Chinese people continue to be unaware and do not wake up, then the shame of being called the "Sick Man of East Asia" will never be erased. It is not only the elimination from the Olympic Games that is shameful. The performance of our country's soccer team in this Olympic Games won profound and accurate criticism. It was said that the first half would be a draw, and in the second half, China would lose two goals. The result was as expected. Good technique is certainly important, but the final judgment of victory or defeat depends on whether physical strength can last. This year, I am serving at the Hongqiao Sanatorium. Because of our country's dismal defeat in the Olympic Games and the full body health checkups conducted at the Hongqiao Sanatorium, I deeply feel the following thoughts.

Full body checkups are an urgent measure for individuals, families, society, and the country. After a checkup, many unconscious diseases can be discovered. The progress of modern medicine and health is rapid. People generally know that treating a disease is not as good as preventing it, and early treatment is better than crying for help when the disease is incurable. According to my experience of more than ten years, patients who come to the hospital for treatment often find that other diseases are progressing at the same time, but the patients are not aware that the hidden dangers are deep and life is approaching its end. They still hope for treatment until it is too late. Alas, the number of sacrifices like this who do not know to undergo full body checkups early is countless.

The procedure for a checkup starts with a general assessment of the whole body, and then proceeds to each organ in order. Whether body temperature, pulse, and breathing are normal, whether blood pressure is elevated, whether body weight and height are suitable for the standard number compared to age, whether nutrition is sufficient, and whether development is complete are not difficult to know after a checkup.

As for each organ, whether the skin has diseases and what the cause is, skin diseases are divided into internal and external causes. How is the vision of the eye, is there the most common trachoma? How is the hearing of the ear, is there pus flowing? Is the inside of the nose normal? Are there any obstacles in the respiratory tract? Are the teeth, the first organ for digesting food, neat and strong? How is the throat? Are the tonsils enlarged? Is there lymph node swelling in the neck? Is the thyroid gland normal? Is the position, size, and sound of the heart in the chest normal? Is the percussion and auscultation of the lungs normal? Are the positions and functions of the spleen, liver, stomach, etc. in the abdomen normal? Is the development of the reproductive organs healthy? Is there a hernia? Is the posture of the whole body abnormal? If so, should it be corrected? All of this can also be known by examination.

For others, such as the erythrocyte sedimentation rate, which can determine the strength of the body's resistance, the Wassermann reaction, which can know the presence or absence of syphilis in the body, the examination of urine, which can know the changes in the body's material metabolism, the examination of stool, which can know the existence of parasites, the examination of sputum, which can know the presence or absence of tuberculosis bacteria, and the thickness of the blood, which can be known by taking a few drops of blood from the finger or ear, are all things that should be paid attention to for overall health.

Common Sense of Hygiene for Ear, Nose, Throat and Eye Diseases

— Tang Renjin

(101) What is Color Blindness?

Human eyes can distinguish all colors because the retina at the back of the eye has a function to distinguish colors. This function is called color vision in medicine. The cone cells in the retina are responsible for color vision. The cone cells are most numerous near the macula of the retina, so their color vision is also the most sensitive. Conversely, in the green part of the retina's edge, color vision is slow. There is a lack of sensitivity to red and green colors. If this color vision is weakened or disappears, it is called color blindness. Medically speaking, color blindness can be divided into two types: congenital and acquired. Namely:

(1) Congenital color blindness – mostly caused by incomplete development.

(2) Acquired color blindness – generally caused by diseases of the retina, choroid, and optic nerve, etc. The two are described separately below. (1) Congenital color blindness – Congenital color blindness usually occurs in both eyes. Its degree varies, some deep and some shallow. When the degree is shallow, the patient finds it slightly difficult to distinguish colors and is often hesitant. When the degree is deep, the patient is almost completely unable to distinguish colors (either red or green). However, color blind patients often do not realize they have any disability. It is not until a physical examination that it can be discovered and proven. Those with complete color vision deficiency are called total color blindness. Those with weakened color vision are called total color weakness. Those with red-green color vision deficiency but healthy blue-yellow color vision are called red-green color blindness. Mild cases are called red-green color weakness. Among them, red-green color blindness and red-green color weakness can each be divided into two: red color blindness and green color blindness, and red color weakness and green color weakness.

Total color blindness and total color weakness are rare eye diseases. The diseased eye of total color blindness cannot sense color at all. As a result, all objects appear gray. Although there are gradations of brightness and darkness, there is no color. Sometimes, there is also photophobia and nystagmus. It is more common in those whose parents are blood relatives. Total color weakness refers to the simultaneous weakening of red-green and blue-yellow color vision.

Red-green color blindness is the most common type of color vision impairment. Four to five percent of men suffer from this disease. One-tenth of women suffer from this disease compared to men. There is also a hereditary relationship.

(2) Acquired color blindness – During various eye diseases, color field defects can often occur. At this time, there is mostly visual impairment and central or green defects in the visual field. Generally, in diseases of the optic nerve, the sensation of red and green is impaired. Red is seen as dark red. Green is seen as green-gray. In diseases of the retina and choroid, blue-yellow is first affected. Blue is seen as black or green. Yellow is seen as white or gray.

The danger of color blindness – The danger of color blindness is completely different depending on the occupation. Ordinary occupations such as doctors, lawyers, accountants, engineers, and those serving in the banking, political, and business worlds are not greatly affected if they are color blind. As for painters and occupations related to pigments, it is already inconvenient and hinders work. The most dangerous are occupations such as captains, pilots, airplane pilots, train drivers, and car drivers. This is because if these professions are color blind, the traffic lights lose their effectiveness immediately. Therefore, danger can occur at any time. Therefore, when conducting physical examinations for these occupations, it is necessary to carefully and thoroughly check for color blindness. If any is found, they should change to other occupations and should never make any compromises.

Common Knowledge Q & A About Diseases

— Cheng Hanzhang

(92) Foreign Objects and Stones in the Bladder

(Q) How can foreign objects exist in the bladder?

Page 18

(A) Because sometimes the catheter is inserted carelessly and breaks or small objects are inserted carelessly due to playing around, causing them to remain in the bladder.

(Q) What are the dangers of foreign objects in the bladder?

(A) It is often the main cause of bladder bleeding or gradually causes the bladder to become ulcerated. It can also become the central nucleus of bladder stones.

(Q) How are bladder stones formed?

(A) The main reason is the descent of kidney stones or the presence of foreign objects as the central nucleus, which are decomposed by alkaline urine, causing calcium phosphate and ammonium urate to adhere to them, gradually becoming larger.

(Q) Among the components of bladder stones, which is more common, phosphate or urate?

(A) Generally, phosphate stones are more common.

(Q) Is there a relationship between age and people with bladder stones?

(A) Many elderly people have them. Some children also have them.

(Q) Is there a relationship with gender?

(A) More men have them than women.

(Q) What symptoms occur when bladder stones develop?

(A) Pain is the main symptom, radiating to the rectum and glans penis. The key is urinary obstruction, interrupted urination. Hematuria also occurs.

(Q) How to diagnose?

(A) For pain, only symptomatic treatment is performed to temporarily stop the pain. The radical cure requires surgical procedures such as lithotripsy and lithotomy.

(Q) Before bladder stones develop, how can we know in advance that there are calcium phosphate and other salts in the urine?

(A) If the urine is often turbid, it can be determined that there are lime salts, which are the elements of stone formation and should be paid attention to as early as possible.

Native Medicinal Plants (Continued)

— Zhou Mengbai

5. Motherwort *Leonurus sibiricus*, L.

(Plant) It grows naturally in the wilderness and is an annual herb. The stem is 1 to 1.5 meters tall. Some plants are hairless throughout, while others have fine hairs. The leaves have long petioles, are pinnately deeply divided, and the segments are linear. The leaf axils have verticillasters. The red-purple labiate flowers bloom in summer. The achenes are trigonous.

(Crude Drug) Motherwort (芜蔚) *Herba Leonri*, is the dried whole plant with flowers collected.

芫蔚子 *Semen Leonuri*, is the seed collected. The surface of the wood product is gray-black and shaped like a slightly elongated particle with three ridges, no more than two millimeters long.

Motherwort means it is effective for treating women's diseases. The plants *L. Cordiacus* and *L.* in the United States, called *Lotherwort*, are also gynecological drugs.

(Ingredients) The leaves contain crystalline substances of Leonuri, 0.5% fatty oil, foul-smelling brain components, resin, etc. Recently, Japanese scientists Kubota and Nakajima isolated a crystalline alkaloid composed of Ci3H2oN4O4, named Leonurin.

(Pharmacology) When Leonurin is injected subcutaneously into 20-day-old mice, it instantaneously causes intermittent spasms, weakens respiration, and eventually causes systemic paralysis, resulting in respiratory silence. After respiratory arrest, the heart continues to beat. The minimum lethal dose for a 20-day-old mouse weighing 1 gram is 0.6-0.7 micrograms. When Lnurin is applied to the isolated uterus of a rabbit, it significantly increases its tension and increases the degree of uterine movement. It also has a diuretic effect.

(Medicinal Use) Old sayings: Motherwort is a hemostatic and tonic for women after childbirth. A single dose is 4-6 grams, used as a decoction. 芫蔚子 is also a diuretic and can treat eye diseases, used as a decoction.

It brightens the eyes, nourishes essence, eliminates water, treats wind, relieves fever, regulates qi. It regulates women's meridians, metrorrhagia and leukorrhea, postpartum and antenatal diseases. Long-term use can help women conceive.

Supplement to the Local News Section of *Shen Bao*

Commentary

Monks Exempt from Civic Training

— Wujue

Monks were once called "bald bandits" by some, but this title is really too broad. Because not every monk is a "bald bandit", so even if they chant scriptures all day long, they are not excluded from citizenship. However, obligations and rights are opposed to each other. Since monks have obtained the rights of citizens, they naturally have to fulfill the obligations of citizens, and undergoing civic training is one of the obligations of citizens. But now, Master Taixu has petitioned the government to cancel civic training for the following reasons:

"Buddhists cherish compassion and abstain from killing. If monks who chant scriptures all day long are made to wield weapons and engage in battlefield life, I am afraid they will not be able to do so. Therefore, I am petitioning for cancellation and requesting that they be given corresponding first aid knowledge. Once something happens, they can serve as rear nurses, which they will be able to do happily. They can also publicize religious doctrines in their spare time, killing two birds with one stone!"

What is this! In the eyes of the monks, this is indeed killing two birds with one stone, but we think that it is not only impossible to "kill two birds with one stone" but will "lose several", even "perish together"! Why? Since Buddhists cherish compassion and abstain from killing, they naturally embrace the "suffering" doctrine of non-resistance to foreign aggression. Even if the enemy points a gun at his chest, he will not fight back. If he accidentally hurts the enemy by fighting back, wouldn't that shake his belief in compassion and violate the precept of abstaining from killing?

But people's hearts are not what they used to be. Compassion and abstaining from killing, although beautiful names, are just names, like peace. No matter how compassionate you are, you cannot move the ruthlessness of others. The reason is very simple: to survive, you must struggle. If you don't struggle, you will only die. So after reading Master Taixu's proposal, I worried for the monks. Because according to this situation, it is not necessarily in the monks' best interest. Even if the monks all have the spirit of "suffering," and die without complaint, they will only make a meaningless sacrifice for the country and the nation!

However, the degree of danger is not limited to this. According to Master Taixu's statement, it is best to give monks first aid knowledge, so that they can serve as rear nurses and publicize religious doctrines in their spare time. Now, let's not discuss whether monks can really perform nursing duties happily, because we know that the best nurses are women. Asking clumsy monks to do women's work is somewhat out of place. And what is most unacceptable is "publicizing religious doctrines!" Although believing in religion is an individual's freedom, in this time when national consciousness needs to be promoted, going to publicize Buddhist ideas of transcending the world to those soldiers who "wield weapons to defend the country," and asking them to "cherish compassion" and "abstain from killing," isn't that intentionally putting the Chinese nation in a position of eternal ruin to be slaughtered by others?

Although we do not want to deliberately find fault with people, we believe that Master Taixu's unrealistic theory, even if spoken unintentionally, also has the appearance of becoming a traitor. We love Taixu, we love the monks who are in the same boat with us, and we feel that this "publicizing religious doctrines" is utterly unacceptable.

Even if we retreat a hundred steps, we admit that monks can be exempted from civic training and can be exempted from battlefield life, but they cannot be nurses, and they must never "publicize religious doctrines" in their spare time to "kill two birds with one stone".

A Visit to Lide Oil Factory, One of China's Four Major Oil Factories

— Xishan

(Special Report from Our Newspaper) China's oil pressing industry plays a significant role in the annual export of goods. Therefore, in the past few years, oil pressing has been a very developed industry. However, currently, under the impact of the economic recession affecting all industries, many oil pressing factories have also suffered significant blows. In order to gain a general understanding of the current state of the oil pressing industry, I made a special trip to the Lide Oil Factory on West Suzhou River Road yesterday for a visit.

Lide Oil Factory is one of China's four major oil factories. Since its establishment, it has a rather long history, so its internal scale is also quite large. When I went to visit, Director Liu of the factory personally received me and first led me into the reception room for a few minutes of rest.

On the four walls of the reception room, many statistical reports on the annual production and export volume of China's oil pressing industry were hung. According to the latest statistics, in Shanghai alone, the number of oil pressing factories, large and small, has decreased from more than 20 to 14, and their total capital is only about one million yuan. As a result, the production volume has also decreased year by year, averaging only 240,000 dan of oil and 680,000 dan of oil cake per year. After I read the above report, Director Liu also showed me the production volume table of the Shanghai oil pressing industry for the past few years. Comparing them, it is clear that the oil pressing industry in Shanghai has also fallen into a state of decline in recent years.

Director Liu told me that the oil pressing industry throughout the country produces many types of oil, the common ones being tung oil, raw oil, soybean oil, castor oil, tea oil, vegetable oil, and more than a dozen others, with the widest sales. However, for business reasons, the factory is currently only producing coconut oil and cottonseed oil. So, first, we went to visit the coconut oil workshop.

The work of pressing coconut oil can be divided into four parts: (1) Raw material sorting: The work of this part is to first gather the transported raw materials in one place. After the workers' inspection and sorting, they are placed into the baking oven. In the baking oven, the coconuts are baked once, then taken out and transferred to the cake making area for the second part of the work. (2) Cake making: The coconuts that have been baked become soft, loose powder. Therefore, they must be made into oil cakes of a specified area before they can be placed in the pressing machine. The workers in this part make the coconuts into rectangular oil cakes, with a common area of about 100 cubic inches. (3) Pressing work: The made oil cakes are placed back into the baking oven to dry. After drying, they are placed in the pressing machine. This type of pressing machine has a great force, and each machine can simultaneously press dozens of the prepared coconut cakes. (4) Filtering work: After the pressing machine presses the coconut cakes, the oil extracted flows entirely into the oil tank. Because the oil still contains impurities, it must undergo a filtering process in the tank to remove the impurities from the oil so that it can become pure coconut oil. Then, it is injected into the storage tank through oil pipes. After the coconut is pressed, the remaining residue becomes extremely hard oil cake. Some of this oil cake is directly packaged for export, while some is ground into powder by a grinder, depending on the supply and demand situation.

The second part of the visit was the cottonseed oil factory. This workshop is divided into two floors. The bottom floor is the raw material storage area for cottonseed oil. The upper floor is the cottonseed sorting and pressing workshop. The process of pressing cottonseed oil is slightly more complicated. Because the cottonseed raw materials are mixed with cotton and other impurities when they are transported, they must undergo a cleaning process before pressing to obtain pure cottonseed. When work begins, the cottonseed raw materials are lifted from the storage area on the bottom floor, bag by bag, into the cotton gin on the upper floor. After the cottonseed passes through the cotton gin, the mixed cotton and impurities are separated from the cottonseed. The pure cottonseed flows separately into the . Like this,

Page 20

, after another filtering process, cottonseed oil is completed.

After the pressing work is completed, another step is to pack it into barrels. After leaving the oil pressing workshop, I went with Director Liu to see the barrel filling situation.

Lide Oil Factory has three huge oil storage tanks, all equipped with oil release valves around them, which can be opened automatically, so the oil filling procedure is simple and convenient. According to Director Liu, several thousand barrels can be filled every day. The weight of the oil in the filled barrels cannot be completely accurate, so it needs to be weighed separately. Also, because the factory is located along the Suzhou River, it has its own ships for transporting the exported barrel oil.

After completing the visit, I feel that if China's oil pressing industry can be revitalized and its production efficiency increased, its future has the potential for extreme development. Because the export of vegetable oil occupies a very important position in China's foreign trade goods.

A Kind Old Man

— Qiying

——Miscellaneous Notes on a Mountain Trip, Part Four

The four of us rode our horses and galloped wildly along the mountain road, regardless of how loudly the old groom shouted behind us to slow down the horses. Although I was not good at riding, I almost slid off the saddle several times while going down the slopes, but I finally used all my strength to overcome these dangers. Gradually, my courage grew, as if I were a skilled rider. Several times, I went ahead of my companions, so the horses galloped even faster. The old groom, walking behind us, was left far, far behind, disappearing into the morning mist of the peaks.

The sunlight gradually leaped from the mountain gorge in the east to the high sky, stretching out its fiery giant hands and tightly grasping this bald, shadeless mountain road; but because of this, the yellow sand rose and filled the way ahead. We were sweating, and the horses were panting. Riding in the saddles, our legs and buttocks felt like they were baking in a fire. At this time, the horses couldn't lift their feet to gallop no matter what. No matter how much we whipped them, they didn't resist; they just opened their mouths wide, constantly gasping for air, and white foam rolled out of their mouths. Sweat soaked their bodies. The thin bones between their thighs stood out high, their bellies deflated, and they looked so weak, as if they had just recovered from a serious illness. These four skinny horses, how old they were! Each of them had a pair of blood-red, tearful eyes, as if they were angrily staring at us, or as if they were pleading with us!

Suddenly, the four of us were moved, and I was reminded of the old groom, who was as weak as the horses and chasing after us. He probably wouldn't be as tired as the horses, unable to lift his weak feet, and fainting in some valley. Or he might be crying to the sky: "Gentlemen, aren't you four horse thieves who have stolen my horses?"

Thinking like this, we sat down on a large rock by the side of the road. If the horses hadn't refused to take another step, we really would have wanted to take the horses back to meet the old groom!

There wasn't any water to drink by the side of the road, and we were almost dying of thirst. It happened to be noon, and the sun was scorching hot. Sitting there, we were all sweating, and thinking of the old groom chasing after us under the scorching sun, we couldn't help but shiver with a feverish chill, and a pang of sadness welled up in our hearts. Watching the sunlight gradually climb over the middle of the sky, and still not seeing a single figure on the road, our hearts were even more flustered. Moreover, we still had to rush to the foot of the mountain ahead to stay overnight today.

It wasn't until the sun had slanted to the west that the old groom appeared at the end of the road in the distance. He was walking hurriedly, his body swaying, as if he were a camel carrying a heavy load. From far away, we could see his fatigue and how anxious he was!

The old man didn't know where he had picked up a tree branch, which he used as a cane, tapping the ground with it step by step. The way he looked made us laugh again. When he saw us appearing by the side of the road, the old man panicked, and his joyful mood reached an unimaginable degree. He hurriedly threw away his cane and ran towards us in a stumbling manner. Without exchanging words with us, he went straight to the four horses, touching their bodies with his hands, smelling their heads with his nose, and caressing their faces with his face... The old man was so happy that he was almost crazy. He muttered to himself, not knowing how to comfort his four hard-working horses. The old man simply forgot his own fatigue. The horses, which were originally weak, suddenly perked up at this time. As if seeing a relative, they wagged their heads and tails at the old groom.

A thought suddenly arose in our hearts. We wondered how the old groom would vent his anger in front of us. We quietly sat aside, waiting for the old man to question all our faults.

But, no one expected that the old man was so kind! He smiled kindly and walked towards us, comforting us like a father: "Gentlemen, you are tired, haha!" He smiled, not daring to approach us: "Gentlemen, I'm sorry to have troubled you and made you wait so long." He raised his head to look at the sun: "Alas! It's getting late, it's all my fault, haha, today..." He didn't dare to continue, took a few steps back, and stood there patiently, waiting for our reply. We were all deeply touched by him and couldn't say a word. This kind old man!

After a while, the old man spoke again with a trembling voice: "Gentlemen, if you don't mind, please come to my humble home for the night. There aren't many people in my family. Tomorrow, I'll make sure you can reach the foot of the mountain when you eat breakfast!"

That night, we stayed overnight in the old groom's home.

Short-Term Elementary School

— Ma Jia

After more than five years of unemployment, I was, in terms of appearance, a spiritually withered fellow. Wandering on the road, I really felt like a timid rat. I avoided the gaze of passers-by, those despicable eyes! They made people angry.

Today, I ran to a friend's school, and seeing my friend was busy, I felt a burst of grief. Alas: people are busy, but I am idle! My friend told me to sit down for a while!" I only felt that the sentence was too ironic.

When my friend finished working, he handed me a cigarette and asked me, "How have you been lately?" I only smiled sadly: "Isn't it the same as before—unemployed?"

My friend was very happy with my answer. He suddenly jumped up from the rattan chair, grabbed my shoulders, and said to me very happily, "Ma Jia! There's a position! Do you want it?"

Like a hungry dog, smelling the scent of beef, I drooled. I quickly replied to my friend: "There's a position? Why wouldn't I want it?"

So my friend told me that their school had a short-term elementary school, and they were short of a teacher. Since I didn't have a job, why not take it? Three hours of class every day, sixteen silver dollars a month. My friend said, "But it's a bit hard!" But for me, that was a "lucrative position"! Hard? Is there anything that doesn't take effort when it comes to eating? (To be continued)

Xing Ruiting's Three Smiles

Linji (1220) 9:05 PM to 10:00 PM

Opening "Qin Liangyu"

The Ming Dynasty is in danger, and the country is falling. Unexpectedly, there is a female general in Sichuan. Qin Liangyu is knowledgeable and talented. It is a pity that this hero does not wear women's clothes. Tracing back to her youth, she received her father's education, and the whole family trained to be a strong city. The siblings share the same strategies. She is a beauty who does not give way to men. Furthermore, Shizhu and Qiancheng seek a phoenix partner. Heroic children marry each other. The couple is a good match. They are a generation of heroes who pass on orders. He advises her husband to dedicate his life to the country and establish meritorious deeds. Seeing that the battlefield sword battle is lining up the army. The military orders are strict. At that time, the situation was chaotic and changeable. United Hearts in Life and Death: A Terrifying Ancient Temple

Mutilated Clay Statues of Gods Sticking Out Their Tongues and Walking

The second studio of Star Motion Picture Company on Avenue Albert has recently been permeated with a rather terrifying atmosphere. It should be clarified that this so-called terror is all based on the psychological effect on those who enter. There are no ghosts or demons that constitute terror, but people who enter often get frightened or even run out, especially when there are few people inside. Now, let me tell you this interesting story from beginning to end!

Ying Yunwei's "United Hearts in Life and Death" is actively in progress. A set of an ancient temple was built by the famous set designer Ma Shouhong. The ancient temple occupies a large part of the studio: dilapidated, desolate, and fragmented walls; a chaotic yard that has been abandoned for a long time; withered trees; a decapitated statue of a god holding a real sword guarding the entrance. Inside the temple, it is very high and spacious but very empty. Gigantic gods stare with their gray-black eyes, covered with dust webs, sitting fiercely in the high niches. Around them are clay gods, some with their hands cut off, some with their heads missing, some still looking like they are about to hit or catch people in the dust, some dragging out foot-long tongues, stretching out thin, long hands as if to pounce over. Ox-headed demons and horse-faced spirits, Black and White Impermanence, although covered by dust and cobwebs, their hideous attitudes are not diminished at all.

Before the set was completed, those ox-headed demons and horse-faced spirits, gigantic gods and strange images, were scattered in the dark corners everywhere. If you walked in unknowingly, and took a look to the east, a glaring monster would be staring at you. A glance to the west would reveal a huge demon! One would often be startled without meaning to be! Especially in the quiet when there are not many people, and the light in the studio is very dim.

Once, the studio was filming the set on the other side, it was Ouyang Yuqian's "Qingming Season." In addition to Liming Hui and Zhao Dan, there was also Miss Li Lilian acting. On this side, a worker was moving a grotesque ghost with a long tongue – because it was made of paper, it was very light and easy to move. However, people could not see it from behind. Li Lilian glanced casually and was shocked to see that the ghost was walking, dragging its tongue. She screamed loudly, even shedding tears. Only when she saw that someone was moving it did she breathe a sigh of relief and pat her chest.

This terrifying ancient temple in "United Hearts in Life and Death" is the residence of a strange revolutionary youth. The so-called strange revolutionary youth is a rather frightening character with a scarred face played by Yuan Muzhi.
